  "DOTA_Tooltip_Ability_t72_upgrade" "T-72 (Object 172M)"
 "DOTA_Tooltip_Ability_t72_upgrade_Description" "The most mass produced tank of the second generation. Adopted in the Armed Forces of the USSR since 1973. T-72 was developed and produced by Uralvagonzavod in Nizhny Tagil. Chief designer of the machine - V. N. Venediktov. Ural is in service with the CIS countries , exported to the states of the Warsaw Pact, Finland, India, Iran, Iraq, Syria. Modifications of the T-72 were produced under license in Yugoslavia (M-84), Poland (PT-91), Czechoslovakia and India, which exported them. "
 "DOTA_Tooltip_Ability_t72_upgrade_bonus_health" "Durability:"

 "DOTA_Tooltip_Ability_t72_2A46" "2A46 (D-81TM)"	
"DOTA_Tooltip_Ability_t72_2А46_Description" "After the adoption of the 2A26 tank gun as part of the armament of the new T-64A and T-72 main tanks, the operating experience revealed the lack of new 125-mm smooth-bore tank guns. Due to the influence of weather factors, the barrel of the gun was subject to curvature, which negatively affected the accuracy of shooting.An unsuccessful design of the recoil devices was also revealed.As a result of thermal expansion in the recoil devices, a mixture of recoil fluid and compensation air was formed, which led to an uneven rollback of the gun and a significant decrease in accuracy. To eliminate the shortcomings, work began on a modernized version of the 2A26 gun.The new gun was developed at OKB-9 under the leadership of V. A. Golubev, and in 1970 the 2A46 tank gun was put into service."

The fundamental difference between the Svir and the Cobra was the anti-jamming semi-automatic laser missile control system. guided weapons 9K120 Svir provides firing of a guided missile during the day from a place and from short stops at ranges from 100 to 4000 m. Almost simultaneously, the 9K119 Reflex complex, which has the same as the Svir , missile 9M119. The complexes Svir and Reflex are distinguished by the control system. In the future, all newly produced tanks of the T-80 family were equipped with these complexes."

	"gu_b6" "Other"
	"gu_helper_1" "<font color='#fc032c'>Introduction : About The Project</font> <br>Guardians of Universe - is a project, in which 2-5 players are required for comfortable game, however solo game is possible. There are many mechanincs and important, but not very clear moments. Not knowing them affects gameplay, their difficulty, and sometimes not-obviousness dissuades users from playing. Goal of this guide is an attempt to explain all little moments of the game.<br> 
	<br>
	<font color='#fc032c'>Introduction : Main problem of the game</font> <br>
		It should be understood that currently game cannot be completed and goal is to achieve the highest wave to gain bigger amounts of MMR. In future, when problem with DotA client crushes will be fixed, a way to win (special quest, most likely). It is unknown when it is going to happen, these crushes are caused by ther DotA itself, not the developer.
	  <br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Game preparations : Choosing Difficulty</font> <br>
		 After all players have established connection they can vote for difficulty level of the upcoming game. Vote is anonymous. There are 3 outcomes of the vote:
			a. Vote has one winner. Game starts on the difficulty selected by majority.
			b. Vote has several winners. Difficulty is randomly selected from list of winners.
			c. No one has voted. Game starts on the Easy difficulty level.
		<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Game preparations : Hero Pick Stage</font> <br>
		
		
		Pick stage starts after vote ends. Heroes are separated in 2 groups - anime heroes and heroes of other game and not universes. Transition between choosing from one of these groups can be done through clicking on the button under list of heroes. Pick stage lasts for 120 seconds, but automatically ends if you have already picked a hero.
		<br><br>Heroes can be conditionally divided in 3 groups by their game goals : physical DD, magical DD and tanks. This specification causes notable division of characters by game roles :
		   <br><br><font color='#bf0404'>Physical DD</font> : charcters, whose main damage dealing method are autoattacks (sometimes - abilities, that deal damage based on attack damage). These heroes usually become junglers instead of defending the base.
			<br><br><font color='#e61cc0'>Magical DD</font> : (later on : casters): characters, whose main damage dealing method is spell damage. Usually these characters defend base, because they have abilities that allow to kill creeps fast even on the first level.
		   <br><br><font color='#77e61c'>Tanks</font> : these characters have problems with dealing damage but they can survive much longer because of their abilities.
			<br><br>Of course, this division is not strict, so any character can play any role, but some have advantage as one. (It is not uncommon to see a <font color='#d9e61c'>Legion Legate</font> picked for solo, because her ultimate allows to sustain without huge amount of gold and still deal damage to kill creeps.)
"
	"gu_helper_2" "<font color='#62fc03'>Beginning of the game : Andromeda</font> <br><br>

	 The game starts after players appear on the map. Main object for players on the map is Andromeda. Her death withholds 1 attempt from team. If players do not have attempts left - game ends with their loss. She can defend herself from 1 and 2 waves, but it requires either Defense or Upgrading. Though upgrading improves her battle capacity, it is a timed solution; best decision is to keep at least one character for Defense. Classic solution - caster.

	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Beginning of the game : Gaining MMR and CU-Point</font> <br><br>

	Players gain MMR (2-6 on Easy, 6-10 on Standard, 10-18 on Hard, 14-26 on Absurd) for completing a wave, starting with 6th. This MMR will be displayed in Profile. You can loose MMR either by killing an ally or leaving a game, for each wave your team completes, you will loose doubled MMR.

	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Beginning of the game : Enemy Description</font> <br><br>

	  Enemy of players are invaders - units who will come in waves in order to kill Andromeda. Their spawn spots are so-called enemy stargates (10 stargates are divided on 3 locations); these gates differ in that their addresses cannot be manually dialed by players. The only mean to teleport to them - quest Random Address (gates are selected randomly).
		Each wave of invaders consists of 40 units - 25 melee and 15 ranged. They come out from enemy stargates in groups of 5.
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Beginning of the game: Tactic</font> <br><br>

	Players appear on the territory of the main location, near Andromeda and home Stargates (later on Base). Three paths lead to Andromeda from different locations, from where enemy comes. Roles differ depending on number of players on the map. At least 1 player must always remain at the base (depending on the difficulty the number may wary). Other players in majority of times move to neutral spots to gain money. It is important that money gained by junglers is shared with all team, so farming neutral spots is beneficial for everyone.
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Beginning of the game : Bying Items</font> <br><br>
	 After gaining enough gold and required items it is a good idea to think about killing bosses to get upgraded items (mainly these are upgraded Guardian Greaves, Demigod Cape 3 и Little Dwarf 2). If players have enough slots and damage they can  kill Overlord of the Universe and get an additional attempt.
	<br><br>
"

	"gu_helper_3" "<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Boss Fight System : Main</font> <br><br>

	 There are 6 bosses that can be summoned by players at any time. Each boss has own abilities. Health, damage, armor and other stats of these bosses grow with number of completed waves. After killing such boss players can choose one item from list of 3 randomized items from respective drop list.
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Boss Fight System : Vote</font> <br><br>
	  After clicking on icon of the desired boss a vote will start. Auto-dialing of the address will start after votes goal is reached. All players will be forcefully teleported to the base.
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Boss Fight System : Reward</font> <br><br>
	After killing a boss players will be forcefully teleported back to the base and after that they will be able to choose a reward.
"

	"gu_helper_4" "<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Choosing Race : IMPORTANT!!!!</font> <br><br>
	Each player can choose a race ONCE. Each race has own unique bonuses that will improve with progression of the rank. You can read more about each race by hovering over icon of the respective race.
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Choosing race : Race progression</font> <br><br>
	  Rank progresses this way:<br>
				Players can progress chosen race only.<br>
				Players can progress race rank only by playing on heroes of this race.<br>
				MMR progress depends on number of the wave and difficulty level (wave number * difficulty level / 2).<br>
				One race rank - 1000 MMR.<br>
				Race MMR is global. This means that all players of this race can affect it.<br>
"

	"gu_helper_5" "<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Introduction</font> <br><br>
	Star Gates System is one of the most important game mechanics, and use of it is one of the most important skills, required for successful walkthrough. The cause is location of different game areas, inaccessible with other travelling methods. Basically, Star Gates - web of stationary teleports, connected with each other.
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Basics</font> <br><br>
	 DHD (Dialling Home Device) is an important part of the System and crucial distinction between different Star Gates on the map. All Gates can be combined in two groups : Gates with DHD and without it. This is one of main game-play differences, because only Gates with DHD can be used as home-point.<br>
	The only mean of travelling between two Gates is dialling of respective symbol order, unique for every Gate - its Address. The amount of Gates, with known unique address, is limited. All such Gates lead to separated locations, required for walkthrough.<br>
		Dialling of a Star Gate Address can be done two ways : manually or automatically. Main functional difference of these two means is that Autodialling requires Energy to work - 200. Manual Dialling does not require Energy, but inexperienced players take more time, which can be crucial in some situations. Address Scrolls - Autodialling analogue, that does not require Energy - can be used to travel to different Neutral Camps and also for returning to the Base.<br>
		Stargate Address Autodialling can be initiated by clicking Profile button in the upper left corner of the screen. Press 'Stargates' in the opened window and select desired destination point. The window will close after that and Autodialling of the Address will start.<br>
		Ibid. in 'Bosses' folder an Epic Boss can be chosen to fight against. If a vote will be successful, Address of Boss Arena Stargate will be autodialled with no charge. Players will be moved to Base Stargate prior to teleportation.<br>
	To manually dial a Stargate Address you need to click on a DHD with M1 (Shift+M1 on Energy Bar for Pegasus Contracts Addresses). After that the Panel will appear, in which a Stargate Addresss can be dialled by sequentially pressing M1 on respective symbols. After dialling a required amount of them a 'DIAL' button will appear in the lower right corner of the window. After clicking it, the dialled Address is checked whether it matches existing Addresses, and if it is correct, the user is teleported to the destination point. While using any of those means, user have to be within range of 1500 units from a DHD! The Panel can be closed by clicking on the cross in the lower left corner of the Panel.<br>
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Advice</font> <br><br>
	Do not come close to a Stargate while an Address is dialled, because an 'energy discharge' occurs in small area around Stargates after an activation, and anybody within the area will recieve 'root' effect for 10 seconds.<br>
		Have at least one teleportation scroll with you, because if you do not know an Address by heart, then you will lose time, trying to dial it.<br>
		Addresses for quests like Random Address have to be dialled manually (autodial is blocked).<br>
		Unlike Autodial, while manually dialling Addresses you do not get invulnerability, so be wary. If you manually dial an address (eg. while completing 'random address' quest) at the base you can be killed by wave mobs. Also be wary after teleportation, since random addresses teleport you to Stargates, that are used by enemy.<br>
"

	"gu_helper_6" "<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>CU-Shop</font> <br><br>
	You can upgrade Andromeda and antennas with CU-Pointsm and also buy heroes Tobiichi Origani and Wind Warrior for CU-Dark Coins. This currency is gained by completing quests Random Address and Random Item (20 and 5 respectively). At the same time CU-Points can be obtained in a certain ammount after completing a wave starting with 6th on any difficulty level.
			It should be noted that upgrading Andromeda and radars lasts only during current game, and values will be reset at the start of the next game.
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Weather</font> <br><br>
	There are different weather conditions in the game. Weather effects are selected randomly for a certain time span. Every weather affects game in its own way.
		   <br> <font color='#62fc03'>Sunny</font> - Sun rays grant additional vision range to the hit hero. <br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Rain</font> - This weather reduces vision range to that of during the night.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Storm</font> - Getting hit by a lightning during the storm will stun the hit hero for 5 seconds.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Snow</font> - This weather does not affect your character at all.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Blizzard</font> - Getting hit by ice blast during the blizzard will root the hit hero for 5 seconds.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Slush</font> - Getting into a swamp greately reduces movespeed and decreases armor by 10.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Sand Storm</font> - This weather reduces your vision range to minimal and also creates sand storms all over the map which will slow heroes and make them miss with attacks.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Time Rift</font> - This weather creates time rifts. Getting into one will give 500 experience.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Blood Rain</font> - Walking through a blood puddle will promptly increase their attack speed.<br>
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Random Quests</font> <br><br>
	There are 3 types of random quests : address dial, random item quest and random boss kill.<br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Address Dial</font> - This quest comes in two variants : Milkyway Stargate Address (7 chevrons) and Pegasus Stargate Address(8 chevrons). Reward for quest is same for both. Quest can be completed only within range of 1500 from a DHD. After successful address dialling player is moved to one of enemy gates(randomly). Aside from rewards shown in the description completing the quest also gives player 20 CU-Dark Coins. Quest duration - 2 minutes.<br><br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Item Quest</font> - An item appears at one of several spots on the map in. Red circle will show its location (the item is located at the center of the circle). Circe will be visible on the mini-map for 1 minute. To pick up the item you have to have a free neutral item slot. Aside from rewards shown in the description completing the quest also gives player 5 CU-Dark Coins. Quest duration - 2 minutes.<br><br>
			<font color='#62fc03'>Random Boss Kill</font> - To complete this quest players have to dial address of the 'Boss Arena' location. After killing a boss you will be rewarded with listed reward (after completing the quest 0 gold and experience is written, because boss drops the reward). Quest duration - 6 minutes.<br><br>
	<br><br><font color='#62fc03'>Unlocking heroes</font> <br><br>
	Part of heroes are locked from the start. Each hero in this category has their own unlocking criteria.<br>
		   <font color='#dec823'>Neptune</font> Use Heal Beam on Andromeda 51 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Aqua</font> Get Useless Goddes from Random Active Skill and use it 2 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Earth Mage</font> Get Stone Throw from Random Active Skill and use it 50 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Kurumi Tokisaki</font> Use item Angel Zafkiel of any grade 100 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Interdimensional Parrot</font> 3000+ of current MMR. If you loose MMR you will loose access to it.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Lina</font> 15000+ of current MMR. If you loose MMR you will loose access to it.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Yumemi Okazaki</font> Kill respective boss in Random Boss Kill or Pegasus Contract 2 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Blackhole-chan</font> Kill respective boss in Random Boss Kill or Pegasus Contract 100 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Emilia</font> Kill respective boss in Random Boss Kill or Pegasus Contract 50 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Clown</font> Kill respective boss in Pegasus Contract 10 times.<br>
			<font color='#dec823'>Sniper</font> Kill respective boss in Pegasus Contract 30 times.<br>
"

Base chance to get 4★ a hero = 13,100%. Getting a 4★ hero is guaranteed at least once in 10 attemts.<br><br>
Base chance to get 3★ a hero = 85,300%.<br><br>
